Generating .MTREE

CMD: bsdtar -czf .MTREE --format=mtree --options=!all,use-set,type,uid,mode,time,size,md5,sha256,link .PKGINFO usr

Tar-ing up files

CMD: bsdtar -cf - .PKGINFO usr .MTREE

CMD: xz -c -z

Successfully ran bsdtar -cf - .PKGINFO usr .MTREE | xz -c -z
